<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="initial-files" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#initial-files"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Initial Files</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultAcceptedFiles</code> prop to set the initial files in the file upload component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="clear-trigger" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#clear-trigger"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Clear Trigger</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">ClearTrigger</code> to remove all uploaded files at once.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="dropzone" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#dropzone"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Dropzone</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Dropzone</code> to enable drag-and-drop. It exposes a <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-dragging</code> attribute for styling.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="directory-upload" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#directory-upload"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Directory Upload</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">directory</code> prop to upload entire folders. Access file paths through <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">file.webkitRelativePath</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_93hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">When uploading directories with many files, set <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">maxFiles</code> to a higher value or remove it entirely to prevent
rejections.</p>
</blockquote>
<h3 id="accepted-file-types" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accepted-file-types"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accepted File Types</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">accept</code> prop to restrict file types. Accepts MIME types (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">image/png</code>) or extensions (<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">.pdf</code>).</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="error-handling" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#error-handling"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Error Handling</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Set constraints with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">maxFiles</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">maxFileSize</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">minFileSize</code>, and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">accept</code>. Rejected files include error codes like
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">TOO_MANY_FILES</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">FILE_INVALID_TYPE</code>, <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">FILE_TOO_LARGE</code>, or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">FILE_EXISTS</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="file-transformations" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#file-transformations"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>File Transformations</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">transformFiles</code> to process files before they&#x27;re added. Useful for image compression, format conversion, or
resizing.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="field" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#field"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Field</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field</code> to add helper text and error handling.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9thanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9thanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9thanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the file upload is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useFileUpload</code> hook. This
way you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_a3hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_a3hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_a3hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="pasting-files" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#pasting-files"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Pasting Files</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">setClipboardFiles</code> to enable pasting images from the clipboard.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_a9hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_a9hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_a9hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="media-capture" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#media-capture"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Media Capture</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">capture</code> to access the device camera. Set to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">&quot;environment&quot;</code> for back camera or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">&quot;user&quot;</code> for front camera.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_afhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_afhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_afhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="rejected-files" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#rejected-files"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Rejected Files</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Access <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">rejectedFiles</code> from the context to display validation errors.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_alhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_alhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_alhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="guides" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#guides"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Guides</h2>
<h3 id="file-previews" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#file-previews"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>File Previews</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">ItemPreview</code> with type matching to show appropriate previews based on file format.</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">type=&quot;image/*&quot;</code>: Shows image thumbnails using <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">ItemPreviewImage</code></li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">type=&quot;video/*&quot;</code>: For video file previews</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">type=&quot;application/pdf&quot;</code>: For PDF files</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">type=&quot;.*&quot;</code>: Generic fallback for any file type</li>
</ul>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.ItemPreview</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> type</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;image/*&quot;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.ItemPreviewImage</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.ItemPreview</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.ItemPreview</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> type</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;video/*&quot;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">VideoIcon</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.ItemPreview</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.ItemPreview</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> type</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;application/pdf&quot;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">PdfIcon</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.ItemPreview</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.ItemPreview</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> type</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&quot;.*&quot;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileIcon</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.ItemPreview</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="disable-dropzone" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#disable-dropzone"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Disable Dropzone</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To disable drag-and-drop functionality, set <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">allowDrop</code> to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">false</code>.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.Root</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> allowDrop</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">false</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">{</span><span style="color:#8B949E">/* ... */</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="prevent-document-drop" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#prevent-document-drop"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Prevent Document Drop</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">By default, we prevent accidental navigation when files are dropped outside the dropzone. Set <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">preventDocumentDrop</code> to
<code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">false</code> to disable this.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.Root</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> preventDocumentDrop</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">false</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">{</span><span style="color:#8B949E">/* ... */</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="prevent-double-open" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#prevent-double-open"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Prevent Double Open</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">disableClick</code> on <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Dropzone</code> when delegating clicks to a nested <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Trigger</code>. This prevents the file picker from
opening twice.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.Dropzone</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> disableClick</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.Trigger</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;Choose Files&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.Trigger</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  Drag files here</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">FileUpload.Dropzone</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>

to enable drag-and-drop. It exposes a `data-dragging` attribute for styling.\n\n**Example: dropzone**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/react/file-upload'\nimport { FileIcon, UploadIcon, XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/file-upload.module.css'\n\nexport const Dropzone = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cFileUpload.Root maxFiles={5} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eFile Upload\u003c/FileUpload.Label\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Dropzone className={styles.Dropzone}\u003e\n      \u003cUploadIcon className={styles.DropzoneIcon} /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.DropzoneContent}\u003e\n        \u003cspan className={styles.DropzoneTitle}\u003eDrag and drop files here\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cspan className={styles.DropzoneDescription}\u003eor click to browse\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Dropzone\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n        {({ acceptedFiles }) =\u003e\n          acceptedFiles.map((file) =\u003e (\n            \u003cFileUpload.Item key={file.name} file={file} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n              \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\"image/*\" className={styles.ItemPreview}\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreviewImage className={styles.ItemPreviewImage} /\u003e\n              \u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n              \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\".*\" className={styles.ItemPreview}\u003e\n                \u003cFileIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n              \u003cFileUpload.ItemName className={styles.ItemName} /\u003e\n              \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText className={styles.ItemSizeText} /\u003e\n              \u003cFileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger className={styles.ItemDeleteTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/FileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n          ))\n        }\n      \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/solid/file-upload'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\n\nexport const Dropzone = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cFileUpload.Root maxFiles={5}\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Label\u003eFile Upload\u003c/FileUpload.Label\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Dropzone\u003eDrag and drop files here\u003c/FileUpload.Dropzone\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n        {(context) =\u003e (\n          \u003cFor each={context().acceptedFiles}\u003e\n            {(file) =\u003e (\n              \u003cFileUpload.Item file={file}\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\"image/*\"\u003e\n                  \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreviewImage /\u003e\n                \u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\".*\"\u003eFile\u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemName /\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText /\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003eX\u003c/FileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003e\n              \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/For\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/vue/file-upload'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cFileUpload.Root :maxFiles=\"5\"\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Label\u003eFile Upload\u003c/FileUpload.Label\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Dropzone\u003e\n      \u003cdiv\u003eDrag and drop files here\u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003cdiv\u003eor click to browse\u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Dropzone\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Context v-slot=\"{ acceptedFiles }\"\u003e\n        \u003cFileUpload.Item v-for=\"file in acceptedFiles\" :file=\"file\" :key=\"file.name\"\u003e\n          \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\"image/*\"\u003e\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreviewImage /\u003e\n          \u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n          \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\".*\"\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003eFile Icon\u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n          \u003cFileUpload.ItemName /\u003e\n          \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText /\u003e\n          \u003cFileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003eX\u003c/FileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/svelte/file-upload'\n  import { FileIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cFileUpload.Root maxFiles={5}\u003e\n  \u003cFileUpload.Label\u003eFile Upload\u003c/FileUpload.Label\u003e\n  \u003cFileUpload.Dropzone\u003eDrag and drop files here\u003c/FileUpload.Dropzone\u003e\n\n  \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n      {#snippet render(fileUpload)}\n        {#each fileUpload().acceptedFiles as file (file.name)}\n          \u003cFileUpload.Item {file}\u003e\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\"image/*\"\u003e\n              \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreviewImage /\u003e\n            \u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\".*\"\u003e\n              \u003cFileIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemName /\u003e\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText /\u003e\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003eX\u003c/FileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003e\n          \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n        {/each}\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n\n  \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Directory Upload\n\nUse the `directory` prop to upload entire folders. Access file paths through `file.webkitRelativePath`.\n\n**Example: directory-upload**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/react/file-upload'\nimport { FileIcon, FolderIcon, XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/file-upload.module.css'\n\nexport const DirectoryUpload = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cFileUpload.Root directory className={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eUpload Folder\u003c/FileUpload.Label\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n      \u003cFolderIcon style={{ width: '1rem', height: '1rem' }} /\u003e\n      Select Folder\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n        {({ acceptedFiles }) =\u003e\n          acceptedFiles.map((file) =\u003e (\n            \u003cFileUpload.Item key={file.name} file={file} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemPreview}\u003e\n                \u003cFileIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003cFileUpload.ItemName className={styles.ItemName}\u003e\n                {file.webkitRelativePath || file.name}\n              \u003c/FileUpload.ItemName\u003e\n              \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText className={styles.ItemSizeText} /\u003e\n              \u003cFileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger className={styles.ItemDeleteTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/FileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003e\n            \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n          ))\n        }\n      \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/solid/file-upload'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\n\nexport const DirectoryUpload = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cFileUpload.Root directory\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Trigger\u003eUpload Folder\u003c/FileUpload.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n        {(fileUpload) =\u003e (\n          \u003cFor each={fileUpload().acceptedFiles}\u003e\n            {(file) =\u003e (\n              \u003cFileUpload.Item file={file}\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemName\u003e{file.webkitRelativePath ?? file.name}\u003c/FileUpload.ItemName\u003e\n              \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/For\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/vue/file-upload'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cFileUpload.Root directory\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Trigger\u003eUpload Folder\u003c/FileUpload.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Context v-slot=\"{ acceptedFiles }\"\u003e\n        \u003cFileUpload.Item v-for=\"file in acceptedFiles\" :file=\"file\" :key=\"file.name\"\u003e\n          \u003cFileUpload.ItemName\u003e{{ file.webkitRelativePath ?? file.name }}\u003c/FileUpload.ItemName\u003e\n        \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/svelte/file-upload'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cFileUpload.Root directory\u003e\n  \u003cFileUpload.Trigger\u003eUpload Folder\u003c/FileUpload.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n      {#snippet render(fileUpload)}\n        {#each fileUpload().acceptedFiles as file (file.name)}\n          \u003cFileUpload.Item {file}\u003e\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemName\u003e\n              {file.webkitRelativePath ?? file.name}\n            \u003c/FileUpload.ItemName\u003e\n          \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n        {/each}\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n  \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n\u003e When uploading directories with many files, set `maxFiles` to a higher value or remove it entirely to prevent\n\u003e rejections.\n\n### Accepted File Types\n\nUse the `accept` prop to restrict file types. Accepts MIME types (`image/png`) or extensions (`.pdf`).\n\n**Example: accepted-file-types**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/react/file-upload'\nimport { AlertCircleIcon, ImageIcon, UploadIcon, XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/file-upload.module.css'\n\nexport const AcceptedFileTypes = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cFileUpload.Root accept=\"image/png,image/jpeg\" className={styles.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eUpload Images (PNG and JPEG only)\u003c/FileUpload.Label\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Dropzone className={styles.Dropzone}\u003e\n      \u003cUploadIcon className={styles.DropzoneIcon} /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.DropzoneContent}\u003e\n        \u003cspan className={styles.DropzoneTitle}\u003eDrop your images here\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cspan className={styles.DropzoneDescription}\u003eOnly PNG and JPEG files\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Dropzone\u003e\n\n    \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n      {({ acceptedFiles, rejectedFiles }) =\u003e (\n        \u003c\u003e\n          {acceptedFiles.length \u003e 0 \u0026\u0026 (\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n              {acceptedFiles.map((file) =\u003e (\n                \u003cFileUpload.Item key={file.name} file={file} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n                  \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\"image/*\" className={styles.ItemPreview}\u003e\n                    \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreviewImage className={styles.ItemPreviewImage} /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n                  \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\".*\" className={styles.ItemPreview}\u003e\n                    \u003cImageIcon /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n                  \u003cFileUpload.ItemName className={styles.ItemName} /\u003e\n                  \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText className={styles.ItemSizeText} /\u003e\n                  \u003cFileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger className={styles.ItemDeleteTrigger}\u003e\n                    \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003e\n                \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n              ))}\n            \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n          )}\n\n          {rejectedFiles.length \u003e 0 \u0026\u0026 (\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n              {rejectedFiles.map((fileRejection) =\u003e (\n                \u003cFileUpload.Item\n                  key={fileRejection.file.name}\n                  file={fileRejection.file}\n                  className={styles.Item}\n                  data-rejected\n                \u003e\n                  \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemPreview}\u003e\n                    \u003cAlertCircleIcon /\u003e\n                  \u003c/div\u003e\n                  \u003cFileUpload.ItemName className={styles.ItemName} /\u003e\n                  \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText className={styles.ItemSizeText} /\u003e\n                  \u003cdiv className={styles.ErrorList}\u003e\n                    {fileRejection.errors.map((error) =\u003e (\n                      \u003cdiv key={error} className={styles.ErrorItem}\u003e\n                        {error}\n                      \u003c/div\u003e\n                    ))}\n                  \u003c/div\u003e\n                \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n              ))}\n            \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n\n    \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/solid/file-upload'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\n\nexport const AcceptedFileTypes = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cFileUpload.Root accept=\"image/png,image/jpeg\"\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Label\u003eFile Upload (PNG and JPEG only)\u003c/FileUpload.Label\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Dropzone\u003eDrop your files here\u003c/FileUpload.Dropzone\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Trigger\u003eSelect Files\u003c/FileUpload.Trigger\u003e\n\n    \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n        {(context) =\u003e (\n          \u003cFor each={context().acceptedFiles}\u003e\n            {(file) =\u003e (\n              \u003cFileUpload.Item file={file}\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemName /\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText /\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003eRemove\u003c/FileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003e\n              \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/For\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n\n    \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n        {(context) =\u003e (\n          \u003cFor each={context().rejectedFiles}\u003e\n            {(fileRejection) =\u003e (\n              \u003cFileUpload.Item file={fileRejection.file}\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemName /\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText /\u003e\n                \u003cdiv\u003e\n                  \u003cFor each={fileRejection.errors}\u003e{(error) =\u003e \u003cdiv style={{ color: 'red' }}\u003e{error}\u003c/div\u003e}\u003c/For\u003e\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n            )}\n          \u003c/For\u003e\n        )}\n      \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n\n    \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/vue/file-upload'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cFileUpload.Root accept=\"image/png,image/jpeg\"\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Label\u003eFile Upload (PNG and JPEG only)\u003c/FileUpload.Label\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Dropzone\u003eDrop your files here\u003c/FileUpload.Dropzone\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Trigger\u003eSelect Files\u003c/FileUpload.Trigger\u003e\n\n    \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Context v-slot=\"{ acceptedFiles }\"\u003e\n        \u003cFileUpload.Item v-for=\"file in acceptedFiles\" :file=\"file\" :key=\"file.name\"\u003e\n          \u003cFileUpload.ItemName /\u003e\n          \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText /\u003e\n          \u003cFileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003eRemove\u003c/FileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003e\n        \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n\n    \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Context v-slot=\"{ rejectedFiles }\"\u003e\n        \u003cFileUpload.Item\n          v-for=\"fileRejection in rejectedFiles\"\n          :file=\"fileRejection.file\"\n          :key=\"fileRejection.file.name\"\n        \u003e\n          \u003cFileUpload.ItemName /\u003e\n          \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText /\u003e\n          \u003cdiv\u003e\n            \u003cdiv v-for=\"error in fileRejection.errors\" :key=\"error\" style=\"color: red\"\u003e\n              {{ error }}\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n      \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n\n    \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/svelte/file-upload'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cFileUpload.Root accept=\"image/png,image/jpeg\"\u003e\n  \u003cFileUpload.Label\u003eFile Upload (PNG and JPEG only)\u003c/FileUpload.Label\u003e\n  \u003cFileUpload.Dropzone\u003eDrop your files here\u003c/FileUpload.Dropzone\u003e\n  \u003cFileUpload.Trigger\u003eSelect Files\u003c/FileUpload.Trigger\u003e\n\n  \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n      {#snippet render(context)}\n        {#each context().acceptedFiles as file (file.name)}\n          \u003cFileUpload.Item {file}\u003e\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemName /\u003e\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText /\u003e\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003eRemove\u003c/FileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003e\n          \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n        {/each}\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n\n  \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n      {#snippet render(context)}\n        {#each context().rejectedFiles as fileRejection (fileRejection.file.name)}\n          \u003cFileUpload.Item file={fileRejection.file}\u003e\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemName /\u003e\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText /\u003e\n            \u003cdiv\u003e\n              {#each fileRejection.errors as error}\n                \u003cdiv style=\"color: red;\"\u003e\n                  {error}\n                \u003c/div\u003e\n              {/each}\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n        {/each}\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n\n  \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Error Handling\n\nSet constraints with `maxFiles`, `maxFileSize`, `minFileSize`, and `accept`. Rejected files include error codes like\n`TOO_MANY_FILES`, `FILE_INVALID_TYPE`, `FILE_TOO_LARGE`, or `FILE_EXISTS`.\n\n**Example: error-handling**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { FileUpload, type FileUploadFileError } from '@ark-ui/react/file-upload'\nimport { AlertCircleIcon, CheckCircleIcon, FileIcon, UploadIcon, XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/file-upload.module.css'\n\nconst errorMessages: Record\u003cFileUploadFileError, string\u003e = {\n  TOO_MANY_FILES: 'Too many files selected (max 3 allowed)',\n  FILE_INVALID_TYPE: 'Invalid file type (only images and PDFs allowed)',\n  FILE_TOO_LARGE: 'File too large (max 1MB)',\n  FILE_TOO_SMALL: 'File too small (min 1KB)',\n  FILE_INVALID: 'Invalid file',\n  FILE_EXISTS: 'File already exists',\n}\n\nexport const ErrorHandling = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cFileUpload.Root\n    maxFiles={3}\n    maxFileSize={1024 * 1024}\n    minFileSize={1024}\n    accept=\"image/*,application/pdf\"\n    className={styles.Root}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eUpload Documents\u003c/FileUpload.Label\u003e\n    \u003cFileUpload.Dropzone className={styles.Dropzone}\u003e\n      \u003cUploadIcon className={styles.DropzoneIcon} /\u003e\n      \u003cdiv className={styles.DropzoneContent}\u003e\n        \u003cspan className={styles.DropzoneTitle}\u003eDrop files here\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cspan className={styles.DropzoneDescription}\u003eImages and PDFs, max 1MB each\u003c/span\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Dropzone\u003e\n\n    \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n      {({ acceptedFiles, rejectedFiles }) =\u003e (\n        \u003c\u003e\n          {acceptedFiles.length \u003e 0 \u0026\u0026 (\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.Section}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.SectionTitle} data-status=\"accepted\"\u003e\n                \u003cCheckCircleIcon\n                  style={{\n                    width: '0.875rem',\n                    height: '0.875rem',\n                    display: 'inline',\n                    marginRight: '0.25rem',\n                    verticalAlign: 'middle',\n                  }}\n                /\u003e\n                Accepted Files\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n                {acceptedFiles.map((file) =\u003e (\n                  \u003cFileUpload.Item key={file.name} file={file} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n                    \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\"image/*\" className={styles.ItemPreview}\u003e\n                      \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreviewImage className={styles.ItemPreviewImage} /\u003e\n                    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n                    \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\"application/pdf\" className={styles.ItemPreview}\u003e\n                      \u003cFileIcon /\u003e\n                    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n                    \u003cFileUpload.ItemName className={styles.ItemName} /\u003e\n                    \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText className={styles.ItemSizeText} /\u003e\n                    \u003cFileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger className={styles.ItemDeleteTrigger}\u003e\n                      \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003e\n                  \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n                ))}\n              \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          )}\n\n          {rejectedFiles.length \u003e 0 \u0026\u0026 (\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.Section}\u003e\n              \u003cdiv className={styles.SectionTitle} data-status=\"rejected\"\u003e\n                \u003cAlertCircleIcon\n                  style={{\n                    width: '0.875rem',\n                    height: '0.875rem',\n                    display: 'inline',\n                    marginRight: '0.25rem',\n                    verticalAlign: 'middle',\n                  }}\n                /\u003e\n                Rejected Files\n              \u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n                {rejectedFiles.map((fileRejection) =\u003e (\n                  \u003cFileUpload.Item\n                    key={fileRejection.file.name}\n                    file={fileRejection.file}\n                    className={styles.Item}\n                    data-rejected\n                  \u003e\n                    \u003cdiv className={styles.ItemPreview}\u003e\n                      \u003cAlertCircleIcon /\u003e\n                    \u003c/div\u003e\n                    \u003cFileUpload.ItemName className={styles.ItemName} /\u003e\n                    \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText className={styles.ItemSizeText} /\u003e\n                    \u003cdiv className={styles.ErrorList}\u003e\n                      {fileRejection.errors.map((error, index) =\u003e (\n                        \u003cdiv key={index} className={styles.ErrorItem}\u003e\n                          {errorMessages[error as FileUploadFileError] || error}\n                        \u003c/div\u003e\n                      ))}\n                    \u003c/div\u003e\n                  \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n                ))}\n              \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n\n    \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { FileUpload, type FileUploadFileError } from '@ark-ui/solid/file-upload'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\n\nconst errorMessages: Record\u003cFileUploadFileError, string\u003e = {\n  TOO_MANY_FILES: '📊 Too many files selected (max 3 allowed)',\n  FILE_INVALID_TYPE: '🚫 Invalid file type (only images and PDFs allowed)',\n ErrorHandling = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cFileUpload.Root\n    maxFiles={3}\n    maxFileSize={1024 * 1024} // 1MB\n    minFileSize={1024} // 1KB\n    accept=\"image/*,application/pdf\"\n  \u003e\n             \u003cFileUpload.Item file={fileRejection.file} class=\"file-item\" data-status=\"rejected\"\u003e\n                    \u003cFileUpload.ItemName /\u003e\n                    \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText /\u003e\n                    \u003cdiv\u003e\n                      \u003cstrong\u003eValidation Errors:\u003c/strong\u003e\n                      \u003cFor \u003c/For\u003e\n                    \u003c/div\u003e\n                  \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n                )}\n              \u003c/For\u003e\n            )\n          }\n        \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n      \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n    \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { FileUpload, type FileUploadFileError } from '@ark-ui/vue/file-upload'\n\nconst errorMessages: Record\u003cFileUploadFileError,   :file=\"file\"\n            :key=\"file.name\"\n            class=\"file-item\"\n            data-status=\"accepted\"\n          \u003e\n            \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n        \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n      \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n\n         \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText /\u003e\n                \u003cdiv\u003e\n                  \u003cstrong\u003eValidation Errors:\u003c/strong\u003e\n                  {#each fileRejection.errors               \u003c/div\u003e\n              \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n            {/each}\n          {/if}\n        {/snippet}\n      \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\n  \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### File Transformations\n\nUse `transformFiles` to process files before they're added. Useful for image compression, format conversion, or\nresizing.\n\n**Example: transform-files**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/react/file-upload'\nimport { compressAccurately } from 'image-conversion'\nimport { ImageIcon, XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/file-upload.module.css'\n\nexport const TransformFiles = () =\u003e {\n  const transformFiles = async (files: File[]) =\u003e {\n    return Promise.all(\n      files.map(async (file) =\u003e {\n        if (file.type.startsWith('image/')) {\n          try {\n            const blob = await compressAccurately(file, 200)\n            return new File([blob], file.name, { type: blob.type })\n          } catch (error) {\n            console.error('Compression failed for:', file.name, error)\n            return file\n          }\n        }\n        return file\n      }),\n    )\n  }\n\n  return (\n    \u003cFileUpload.Root accept=\"image/*\" maxFiles={5} transformFiles={transformFiles} className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Label className={styles.Label}\u003eUpload with Compression\u003c/FileUpload.Label\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Trigger className={styles.Trigger}\u003e\n        \u003cImageIcon style={{ width: '1rem', height: '1rem' }} /\u003e\n        Choose Images\n      \u003c/FileUpload.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup className={styles.ItemGroup}\u003e\n        \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n          {({ acceptedFiles }) =\u003e\n            acceptedFiles.map((file) =\u003e (\n              \u003cFileUpload.Item key={file.name} file={file} className={styles.Item}\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\"image/*\" className={styles.ItemPreview}\u003e\n                  \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreviewImage className={styles.ItemPreviewImage} /\u003e\n                \u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemName className={styles.ItemName} /\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText className={styles.ItemSizeText} /\u003e\n                \u003cFileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger className={styles.ItemDeleteTrigger}\u003e\n                  \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n                \u003c/FileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003e\n              \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n            ))\n          }\n        \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n      \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/solid/file-upload'\nimport { compressAccurately } from 'image-conversion'\nimport { For } from 'solid-js'\n\nexport const TransformFiles = () =\u003e {\n  const transformFiles = async (files: File[]) =\u003e {\n    return Promise.all(\n      files.map(async (file) =\u003e {\n        if (file.type.startsWith('image/')) {\n          try {\n            const blob = await compressAccurately(file, 200)\n            return new File([blob], file.name, { type: blob.type })\n          } catch (error) {\n            console.error('Compression failed for:', file.name, error)\n            return file\n          }\n        }\n        return file\n      }),\n    )\n  }\n\n  return (\n    \u003cFileUpload.Root accept=\"image/*\" maxFiles={5} transformFiles={transformFiles}\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Label\u003eFile Upload with Compression\u003c/FileUpload.Label\u003e\n      \u003cFileUpload.Trigger\u003eChoose Images\u003c/FileUpload.Trigger\u003e\n\n      \u003cFileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n        \u003cFileUpload.Context\u003e\n          {(fileUpload) =\u003e (\n            \u003cFor each={fileUpload().acceptedFiles}\u003e\n              {(file) =\u003e (\n                \u003cFileUpload.Item file={file} class=\"file-item\"\u003e\n                  \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreview type=\"image/*\"\u003e\n                    \u003cFileUpload.ItemPreviewImage /\u003e\n                  \u003c/FileUpload.ItemPreview\u003e\n                  \u003cFileUpload.ItemName /\u003e\n                  \u003cFileUpload.ItemSizeText /\u003e\n                  \u003cFileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003eRemove\u003c/FileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003e\n                \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n              )}\n            \u003c/For\u003e\n          )}\n        \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n      \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n\n      \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { FileUpload } from \u003cFileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003eX\u003c/FileUpload.ItemDeleteTrigger\u003e\n          \u003c/FileUpload.Item\u003e\n        {/each}\n      {/snippet}\n    \u003c/FileUpload.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/FileUpload.ItemGroup\u003e\n\n  \u003cFileUpload.HiddenInput /\u003e\n\u003c/FileUpload.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Field\n\nUse `Field` to add helper text and error handling.\n\n**Example: with-field**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/react/field'\nimport { FileUpload } from '@ark-ui/react/file-upload'\nimport { FileIcon, UploadIcon, XIcon } from
